export default function Documents() {
  // 从 URL 参数读取当前步骤和选中模版
  const routerParams = useMemo(() => {
    const instance = Taro.getCurrentInstance()
    return instance?.router?.params || {}
  }, [])

  const currentStep = useMemo(() => routerParams.step || 'list', [routerParams])
  const templateId = useMemo(() => routerParams.templateId || '', [routerParams])

  // 根据 URL 参数中的 templateId 查找模版
  const selectedTemplate = useMemo(() => {
    if (!templateId) return null
    return TEMPLATES.find(t => t.id === templateId) || null
  }, [templateId])

  const [formData, setFormData] = useState<Record<string, string>>({})
  const [generating, setGenerating] = useState(false)
  const [generatedDoc, setGeneratedDoc] = useState(() => {
    // 从 storage 恢复生成的文书（结果步骤时读取）
    if (currentStep === 'result') {
      try { return Taro.getStorageSync('document_result') || '' } catch { return '' }
    }
    return ''
  })
  const [disputeContent, setDisputeContent] = useState('')
  const [loadingDispute, setLoadingDispute] = useState(false)
  const [showDispute, setShowDispute] = useState(false)

  const setField = (key: string, value: string) => {
    setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, [key]: value }))
  }

  const handleGenerate = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!selectedTemplate) return
    const missingFields = selectedTemplate.fields
      .filter(f => f.required && !formData[f.key]?.trim())
      .map(f => f.label)

    if (missingFields.length > 0) {
      Taro.showToast({ title: `请填写：${missingFields[0]}`, icon: 'none' })
      return
    }

    setGenerating(true)
    try {
      const fieldStr = selectedTemplate.fields
        .map(f => `${f.label}：${formData[f.key] || '（未填写）'}`)
        .join('\n')

      const prompt = `${selectedTemplate.prompt}\n${fieldStr}\n\n请生成完整规范的法律文书，格式清晰，符合法律规范。`

      const { data, error } = await callEdgeFunction<{ content?: string }>('legal-chat', {
        body: { messages: [{ role: 'user', content: prompt }], mode: 'document' },
      })

      if (error) {
        console.error('文书生成错误:', error.message)
        Taro.showToast({ title: '生成失败，请稍后重试', icon: 'none' })
        return
      }
      const doc = data?.content || ''
      // 将结果存入 storage，再跳转到结果页
      Taro.setStorageSync('document_result', doc)
      Taro.setStorageSync('document_template_name', selectedTemplate.name)
      // redirectTo 替换当前表单页，跳转到结果页
      Taro.redirectTo({ url: `/pages/document/index?step=result&templateId=${selectedTemplate.id}` })
    } catch {
      Taro.showToast({ title: '网络异常，请稍后重试', icon: 'none' })
    } finally {
      setGenerating(false)
    }
  }, [selectedTemplate, formData])

  const handleSimulateDispute = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!generatedDoc) return
    const templateName = Taro.getStorageSync('document_template_name') || '法律文书'
    setLoadingDispute(true)
    setShowDispute(true)
    try {
      const prompt = `我已发出以下《${templateName}》：\n\n${generatedDoc.substring(0, 500)}\n\n请模拟对方（房东/雇主/中介）可能的狡辩，并教我如何拆招。`
      const { data, error } = await callEdgeFunction<{ content?: string }>('legal-chat', {
        body: { messages: [{ role: 'user', content: prompt }], mode: 'dispute' },
      })
      if (error) {
        Taro.showToast({ title: '模拟失败，请重试', icon: 'none' })
        setShowDispute(false)
        return
      }
      setDisputeContent(data?.content || '')
    } catch {
      Taro.showToast({ title: '网络异常，请稍后重试', icon: 'none' })
      setShowDispute(false)
    } finally {
      setLoadingDispute(false)
    }
  }, [generatedDoc])

  const copyDoc = () => {
    Taro.setClipboardData({
      data: generatedDoc,
      success: () => Taro.showToast({ title: '已复制到剪贴板', icon: 'success' }),
    })
  }

  const goBackToList = () => {
    // 清除缓存并返回模版列表
    Taro.removeStorageSync('document_result')
    Taro.removeStorageSync('document_template_name')
    Taro.navigateBack({ delta: 99 })
  }

  const disputeParsed = disputeContent ? parseDisputeReply(disputeContent) : null

  // 结果页面
  if (currentStep === 'result') {
    const templateName = Taro.getStorageSync('document_template_name') || '法律文书'
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-background">
        <div className="px-4 py-4">
          <div className="bg-card rounded-2xl border border-border p-4 mb-4">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
              <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground">生成结果</p>
              <span className="text-xl px-2 py-1 bg-secondary text-primary rounded">{templateName}</span>
            </div>
            <div className="border border-border rounded-xl p-4 bg-background">
              <p className="text-xl text-foreground leading-loose whitespace-pre-wrap">{generatedDoc}</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          {!showDispute && (
            <button
              type="button"
              className="flex items-center justify-center leading-none gap-2 border border-primary bg-background rounded-xl w-full mb-3"
              onClick={handleSimulateDispute}
            >
              <div className="py-4 flex items-center gap-2">
                <div className="i-mdi-shield-sword-outline text-2xl text-primary" />
                <span className="text-xl text-primary">学长模拟：对方会怎么狡辩？</span>
              </div>
            </button>
          )}

          {showDispute && (
            <div className="bg-card rounded-2xl border border-border mb-4 overflow-hidden">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-3 border-b border-border">
                <div className="i-mdi-sword-cross text-xl text-primary" />
                <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground">见招拆招</p>
              </div>
              {loadingDispute ? (
                <div className="p-4 flex flex-col gap-2">
                  <div className="skeleton h-4 rounded" />
                  <div className="skeleton h-4 rounded w-5/6" />
                  <div className="skeleton h-4 rounded w-4/6" />
                </div>
              ) : disputeParsed && (
                <div className="p-4 flex flex-col gap-4">
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-xl font-medium text-destructive mb-2">对方可能的狡辩</p>
                    <p className="text-xl text-foreground leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-wrap">{disputeParsed.args}</p>
                  </div>
                  {disputeParsed.counter && (
                    <div>
                      <p className="text-xl font-medium text-primary mb-2">学长教你怎么拆招</p>
                      <div className="law-quote">
                        <p className="text-xl text-foreground leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-wrap">{disputeParsed.counter}</p>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          )}

          <div className="flex flex-col gap-3">
            <button
              type="button"
              className="flex items-center justify-center leading-none gap-2 bg-primary rounded-xl"
              onClick={copyDoc}
            >
              <div className="py-4 flex items-center gap-2">
                <div className="i-mdi-content-copy text-2xl text-primary-foreground" />
                <span className="text-xl text-primary-foreground">复制文书内容</span>
              </div>
            </button>
            <button
              type="button"
              className="flex items-center justify-center leading-none gap-2 border border-border bg-background rounded-xl"
              onClick={goBackToList}
            >
              <div className="py-4 flex items-center gap-2">
                <div className="i-mdi-refresh text-2xl text-foreground" />
                <span className="text-xl text-foreground">重新选择模板</span>
              </div>
            </button>
          </div>
          <div className="mt-4 flex items-start gap-2 px-4 py-3 bg-muted rounded-xl">
            <div className="i-mdi-information-outline text-xl text-muted-foreground flex-shrink-0 mt-0.5" />
            <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">本回复由AI生成，仅供参考，不构成正式法律建议。若情况紧急请咨询专业律师。</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    )
  }

  // 表单填写页面
  if (currentStep === 'form' && selectedTemplate) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-background">
        <div className="px-4 py-4">
          <div className="bg-card rounded-2xl border border-border p-4 mb-4">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-4">
              <div className={`${selectedTemplate.icon} text-3xl text-primary`} />
              <div>
                <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground">{selectedTemplate.name}</p>
                <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground">{selectedTemplate.desc}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
              {selectedTemplate.fields.map((field) => (
                <div key={field.key}>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-1 mb-2">
                    <span className="text-xl text-foreground">{field.label}</span>
                    {field.required && <span className="text-xl text-destructive">*</span>}
                  </div>
                  <div className="border border-input rounded-lg px-4 py-3 bg-background overflow-hidden">
                    <input
                      className="w-full text-xl text-foreground bg-transparent outline-none"
                      placeholder={field.placeholder}
                      value={formData[field.key] || ''}
                      onInput={(e) => { const ev = e as any; setField(field.key, ev.detail?.value ?? ev.target?.value ?? '') }}
                    />
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="flex flex-col gap-3">
            <button
              type="button"
              className="flex items-center justify-center leading-none bg-primary rounded-xl"
              style={{ opacity: generating ? 0.5 : 1 }}
              onClick={handleGenerate}
            >
              <div className="py-4 flex items-center gap-2">
                {generating ? (
                  <div className="i-mdi-loading text-2xl text-primary-foreground animate-spin" />
                ) : (
                  <div className="i-mdi-file-document-edit-outline text-2xl text-primary-foreground" />
                )}
                <span className="text-xl text-primary-foreground">{generating ? '生成中...' : '生成文书'}</span>
              </div>
            </button>
            <button
              type="button"
              className="flex items-center justify-center leading-none border border-border bg-background rounded-xl"
              onClick={() => Taro.navigateBack()}
            >
              <div className="py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
                <div className="i-mdi-arrow-left text-2xl text-foreground" />
                <span className="text-xl text-foreground">返回选择模板</span>
              </div>
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    )
  }

  // 模板选择页面（默认）
  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background">
      <div className="px-4 py-4">
        <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground mb-4">选择需要生成的文书类型</p>
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-3">
          {TEMPLATES.map((template) => (
            <div
              key={template.id}
              className="bg-card rounded-2xl border border-border p-4 flex items-center gap-4 transition-all active:scale-95"
              onClick={() => Taro.navigateTo({ url: `/pages/document/index?step=form&templateId=${template.id}` })}
            >
              <div className={`${template.icon} text-3xl text-primary flex-shrink-0`} />
              <div className="flex-1">
                <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground">{template.name}</p>
                <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground mt-1">{template.desc}</p>
              </div>
              <div className="i-mdi-chevron-right text-2xl text-muted-foreground" />
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

  const [selectedScenario, setSelectedScenario] = useState<Scenario | null>(null)

      if (next.has(key)) next.delete(key)
      else next.add(key)
      return next
    })

        return

      Taro.showToast({ title: '网络异常，请稍后重试', icon: 'none' })

      setLoadingAi(false)
    }

              <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground">共 {selectedScenario.evidences.length} 项证据，已勾选 {checked.size} 项</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* 进度条 */}
          <div className="mb-4">
            <div className="flex justify-between mb-1">
              <span className="text-xl text-foreground">关键证据：{checkedCritical}/{criticalCount}</span>
              <span className={`text-xl font-medium ${readyPercent >= 80 ? 'text-primary' : readyPercent >= 50 ? 'text-amber-600' : 'text-destructive'}`}>
                {readyPercent}% 已备齐
              </span>
            </div>
            <div className="h-2 bg-muted rounded-full overflow-hidden">
              <div
                className={`h-full rounded-full transition-all ${readyPercent >= 80 ? 'bg-primary' : readyPercent >= 50 ? 'bg-amber-400' : 'bg-destructive'}`}
                style={{ width: `${readyPercent}%` }}
              />
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* 证据列表 */}
          {(['critical', 'important', 'helpful'] as const).map(importance => {
            const items = selectedScenario.evidences.filter(e => e.importance === importance)
            const config = IMPORTANCE_CONFIG[importance]
            return (
              <div key={importance} className="mb-4">
                <p className={`text-xl font-medium ${config.color} mb-2`}>{config.label}</p>
                {items.map(item => (
                  <div
                    key={item.key}
                    className={`flex items-start gap-3 px-4 py-3 rounded-xl border mb-2 transition-all ${checked.has(item.key) ? 'border-primary bg-secondary' : `${config.bg} ${config.border}`}`}
                    onClick={() => toggleCheck(item.key)}
                  >
                    <div className={`w-6 h-6 rounded-full border-2 flex-shrink-0 mt-0.5 flex items-center justify-center transition-all ${checked.has(item.key) ? 'border-primary bg-primary' : 'border-muted-foreground bg-transparent'}`}>
                      {checked.has(item.key) && <div className="i-mdi-check text-xl text-primary-foreground" />}
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex-1">
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <div className={`${item.icon} text-xl ${checked.has(item.key) ? 'text-primary' : 'text-muted-foreground'}`} />
                        <p className={`text-xl font-medium ${checked.has(item.key) ? 'text-primary' : 'text-foreground'}`}>{item.label}</p>
                      </div>
                      <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground mt-1 leading-relaxed">{item.desc}</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            )
          })}

          {/* AI建议 */}
          <button
            type="button"
            className="flex items-center justify-center leading-none gap-2 w-full bg-primary rounded-xl mb-3"
            style={{ opacity: loadingAi ? 0.5 : 1 }}

              ) : (

              )}
              <span className="text-xl text-primary-foreground">{loadingAi ? '分析中...' : '学长帮我评估证据'}</span>

              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-3">

                <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground">学长的证据建议</p>
              </div>
              <p className="text-xl text-foreground leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-wrap">{aiSuggestion}</p>
              <div className="flex items-start gap-2 mt-3 px-3 py-2 bg-muted rounded-xl">

        </div>

    )

    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background">
      <div className="px-4 py-4">
        <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground mb-6 leading-relaxed">大学生维权最常见的失败原因就是没有证据。选择你的场景，学长帮你逐一核对必要证据。</p>
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-3">
          {SCENARIOS.map(scenario => (
            <div
              key={scenario.id}
              className="bg-card rounded-2xl border border-border p-4 flex items-center gap-4 transition-all active:scale-95"
              onClick={() => { setSelectedScenario(scenario); setChecked(new Set()) }}
            >
              <div className={`${scenario.icon} text-3xl text-primary flex-shrink-0`} />
              <div className="flex-1">
                <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground">{scenario.name}</p>
                <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground mt-1">
                  {scenario.evidences.filter(e => e.importance === 'critical').length} 项关键证据 · {scenario.evidences.length} 项总清单
                </p>
              </div>
              <div className="i-mdi-chevron-right text-2xl text-muted-foreground" />
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

New String: ```
export default function Evidence() {
  // 从 URL 参数读取当前步骤和场景 ID
  const routerParams = useMemo(() => {
    const instance = Taro.getCurrentInstance()
    return instance?.router?.params || {}
  }, [])

  const currentStep = useMemo(() => routerParams.step || 'list', [routerParams])
  const scenarioId = useMemo(() => routerParams.scenarioId || '', [routerParams])

  // 根据 URL 参数查找场景
  const selectedScenario = useMemo(() => {
    if (!scenarioId) return null
    return SCENARIOS.find(s => s.id === scenarioId) || null
  }, [scenarioId])

  const [checked, setChecked] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set())
  const [aiSuggestion, setAiSuggestion] = useState('')
  const [loadingAi, setLoadingAi] = useState(false)

  const toggleCheck = (key: string) => {
    setChecked(prev => {
      const next = new Set(prev)
      if (next.has(key)) next.delete(key)
      else next.add(key)
      return next
    })
  }

  const handleGetAdvice = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!selectedScenario) return
    const allEvidence = selectedScenario.evidences
    const have = allEvidence.filter(e => checked.has(e.key)).map(e => e.label)
    const missing = allEvidence.filter(e => !checked.has(e.key))
    const criticalMissing = missing.filter(e => e.importance === 'critical').map(e => e.label)

    if (missing.length === 0) {
      Taro.showToast({ title: '证据已齐全，可以维权了！', icon: 'success' })
      return
    }

    setLoadingAi(true)
    setAiSuggestion('')
    try {
      const prompt = `我在处理"${selectedScenario.name}"的维权问题。\n\n已有证据：${have.length > 0 ? have.join('、') : '暂无'}\n关键证据缺失：${criticalMissing.join('、') || '无'}\n\n请针对我的具体情况：\n1. 评估当前证据的充分程度\n2. 指出最紧迫需要补充的证据及采集方法\n3. 给出1-2条立即可行的证据采集建议`

      const { data, error } = await callEdgeFunction<{ content?: string }>('legal-chat', {
        body: { messages: [{ role: 'user', content: prompt }], mode: 'chat' },
      })
      if (error) {
        Taro.showToast({ title: '获取建议失败', icon: 'none' })
        return
      }
      const rawContent: string = data?.content || ''
      const mainContent = rawContent.split('---法律依据---')[0].replace('[结论与分析]', '').trim()
      setAiSuggestion(mainContent)
    } catch {
      Taro.showToast({ title: '网络异常，请稍后重试', icon: 'none' })
    } finally {
      setLoadingAi(false)
    }
  }, [selectedScenario, checked])

  // 证据清单页（step=detail）
  if (currentStep === 'detail' && selectedScenario) {
    const criticalCount = selectedScenario.evidences.filter(e => e.importance === 'critical').length
    const checkedCritical = selectedScenario.evidences.filter(e => e.importance === 'critical' && checked.has(e.key)).length
    const readyPercent = Math.round((checked.size / selectedScenario.evidences.length) * 100)

    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-background">
        <div className="px-4 py-4">
          {/* 场景标题 */}
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-4">
            <div className={`${selectedScenario.icon} text-3xl text-primary`} />
            <div>
              <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground">{selectedScenario.name}</p>
              <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground">共 {selectedScenario.evidences.length} 项证据，已勾选 {checked.size} 项</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* 进度条 */}
          <div className="mb-4">
            <div className="flex justify-between mb-1">
              <span className="text-xl text-foreground">关键证据：{checkedCritical}/{criticalCount}</span>
              <span className={`text-xl font-medium ${readyPercent >= 80 ? 'text-primary' : readyPercent >= 50 ? 'text-amber-600' : 'text-destructive'}`}>
                {readyPercent}% 已备齐
              </span>
            </div>
            <div className="h-2 bg-muted rounded-full overflow-hidden">
              <div
                className={`h-full rounded-full transition-all ${readyPercent >= 80 ? 'bg-primary' : readyPercent >= 50 ? 'bg-amber-400' : 'bg-destructive'}`}
                style={{ width: `${readyPercent}%` }}
              />
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* 证据列表 */}
          {(['critical', 'important', 'helpful'] as const).map(importance => {
            const items = selectedScenario.evidences.filter(e => e.importance === importance)
            const config = IMPORTANCE_CONFIG[importance]
            return (
              <div key={importance} className="mb-4">
                <p className={`text-xl font-medium ${config.color} mb-2`}>{config.label}</p>
                {items.map(item => (
                  <div
                    key={item.key}
                    className={`flex items-start gap-3 px-4 py-3 rounded-xl border mb-2 transition-all ${checked.has(item.key) ? 'border-primary bg-secondary' : `${config.bg} ${config.border}`}`}
                    onClick={() => toggleCheck(item.key)}
                  >
                    <div className={`w-6 h-6 rounded-full border-2 flex-shrink-0 mt-0.5 flex items-center justify-center transition-all ${checked.has(item.key) ? 'border-primary bg-primary' : 'border-muted-foreground bg-transparent'}`}>
                      {checked.has(item.key) && <div className="i-mdi-check text-xl text-primary-foreground" />}
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex-1">
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                        <div className={`${item.icon} text-xl ${checked.has(item.key) ? 'text-primary' : 'text-muted-foreground'}`} />
                        <p className={`text-xl font-medium ${checked.has(item.key) ? 'text-primary' : 'text-foreground'}`}>{item.label}</p>
                      </div>
                      <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground mt-1 leading-relaxed">{item.desc}</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            )
          })}

          {/* AI建议 */}
          <button
            type="button"
            className="flex items-center justify-center leading-none gap-2 w-full bg-primary rounded-xl mb-3"
            style={{ opacity: loadingAi ? 0.5 : 1 }}
            onClick={handleGetAdvice}
          >
            <div className="py-4 flex items-center gap-2">
              {loadingAi ? (
                <div className="i-mdi-loading text-2xl text-primary-foreground animate-spin" />
              ) : (
                <div className="i-mdi-robot-outline text-2xl text-primary-foreground" />
              )}
              <span className="text-xl text-primary-foreground">{loadingAi ? '分析中...' : '学长帮我评估证据'}</span>
            </div>
          </button>

          {aiSuggestion && (
            <div className="bg-card rounded-2xl border border-border p-4 mb-3">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-3">
                <div className="i-mdi-robot-outline text-xl text-primary" />
                <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground">学长的证据建议</p>
              </div>
              <p className="text-xl text-foreground leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-wrap">{aiSuggestion}</p>
              <div className="flex items-start gap-2 mt-3 px-3 py-2 bg-muted rounded-xl">
                <div className="i-mdi-information-outline text-xl text-muted-foreground flex-shrink-0 mt-0.5" />
                <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">{DISCLAIMER}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          <button
            type="button"
            className="flex items-center justify-center leading-none gap-2 w-full border border-border bg-background rounded-xl"
            onClick={() => Taro.navigateBack()}
          >
            <div className="py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
              <div className="i-mdi-arrow-left text-2xl text-foreground" />
              <span className="text-xl text-foreground">返回选择场景</span>
            </div>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    )
  }

  // 场景选择页（默认）
  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background">
      <div className="px-4 py-4">
        <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground mb-6 leading-relaxed">大学生维权最常见的失败原因就是没有证据。选择你的场景，学长帮你逐一核对必要证据。</p>
        <div className="flex flex-col gap-3">
          {SCENARIOS.map(scenario => (
            <div
              key={scenario.id}
              className="bg-card rounded-2xl border border-border p-4 flex items-center gap-4 transition-all active:scale-95"
              onClick={() => Taro.navigateTo({ url: `/pages/evidence/index?step=detail&scenarioId=${scenario.id}` })}
            >
              <div className={`${scenario.icon} text-3xl text-primary flex-shrink-0`} />
              <div className="flex-1">
                <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground">{scenario.name}</p>
                <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground mt-1">
                  {scenario.evidences.filter(e => e.importance === 'critical').length} 项关键证据 · {scenario.evidences.length} 项总清单
                </p>
              </div>
              <div className="i-mdi-chevron-right text-2xl text-muted-foreground" />
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}
```

      Taro.switchTab({ url: path })
    } else {

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on the file: /workspace/app-bar9rto6gwsh/src/pages/calculator/index.tsx:
     1 import { useState, useMemo } from 'react'
     2 import Taro from '@tarojs/taro'
     3 
     4 type CalcType = 'sick' | 'penalty'
     5 
     6 // 病假工资计算
     7 function calcSickWage(params: {
     8   baseSalary: number
     9   sickDays: number
    10   workingDays: number
    11   workYears: number
    12 }): { result: number; detail: string } {
    13   const { baseSalary, sickDays, workingDays, workYears } = params
    14   if (!baseSalary || !sickDays || !workingDays) return { result: 0, detail: '' }
    15 
    16   // 病假工资系数（按工龄）
    17   let ratio = 0.6
    18   if (workYears >= 20) ratio = 1.0
    19   else if (workYears >= 10) ratio = 0.9
    20   else if (workYears >= 5) ratio = 0.8
    21   else if (workYears >= 2) ratio = 0.7
    22 
    23   const dailyWage = baseSalary / workingDays
    24   const sickWage = dailyWage * sickDays * ratio
    25 
    26   const detail = `日薪 = ${baseSalary} ÷ ${workingDays} = ${dailyWage.toFixed(2)} 元\n病假工资系数 = ${(ratio * 100).toFixed(0)}%（工龄${workYears}年）\n病假工资 = ${dailyWage.toFixed(2)} × ${sickDays} × ${(ratio * 100).toFixed(0)}% = ${sickWage.toFixed(2)} 元`
    27 
    28   return { result: sickWage, detail }
    29 }
    30 
    31 // 违约金计算
    32 function calcPenalty(params: {
    33   monthlyRent: number
    34   contractMonths: number
    35   remainMonths: number
    36   penaltyType: 'fixed' | 'ratio'
    37   penaltyValue: number
    38 }): { result: number; detail: string } {
    39   const { monthlyRent, contractMonths, remainMonths, penaltyType, penaltyValue } = params
    40   if (!monthlyRent || !remainMonths) return { result: 0, detail: '' }
    41 
    42   let penalty = 0
    43   let detail = ''
    44 
    45   if (penaltyType === 'fixed') {
    46     penalty = penaltyValue
    47     detail = `固定违约金：${penaltyValue} 元`
    48   } else {
    49     // 按月租金比例
    50     penalty = monthlyRent * penaltyValue
    51     detail = `违约金 = ${monthlyRent} × ${penaltyValue} 月 = ${penalty.toFixed(2)} 元`
    52   }
    53 
    54   const legalMaxPenalty = monthlyRent * remainMonths * 0.3
    55   detail += `\n\n法律提示：违约金通常不超过剩余租金的30%（约${legalMaxPenalty.toFixed(0)}元），超出部分可申请法院调减。`
    56 
    57   if (contractMonths > 0 && remainMonths > contractMonths) {
    58     detail += '\n注意：剩余月数超过合同总月数，请检查输入。'
    59   }
    60 
    61   return { result: penalty, detail }
    62 }
    63 
    64 export default function Calculator() {
    65   const routerParams = useMemo(() => {
    66     const instance = Taro.getCurrentInstance()
    67     return instance?.router?.params || {}
    68   }, [])
    69 
    70   const defaultType: CalcType = (routerParams.type as CalcType) === 'penalty' ? 'penalty' : 'sick'
    71   const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<CalcType>(defaultType)
    72 
    73   // 病假工资
    74   const [baseSalary, setBaseSalary] = useState('')
    75   const [sickDays, setSickDays] = useState('')
    76   const [workingDays, setWorkingDays] = useState('21.75')
    77   const [workYears, setWorkYears] = useState('')
    78 
    79   // 违约金
    80   const [monthlyRent, setMonthlyRent] = useState('')
    81   const [contractMonths, setContractMonths] = useState('')
    82   const [remainMonths, setRemainMonths] = useState('')
    83   const [penaltyType, setPenaltyType] = useState<'fixed' | 'ratio'>('ratio')
    84   const [penaltyValue, setPenaltyValue] = useState('')
    85 
    86   const sickResult = useMemo(() => {
    87     const b = parseFloat(baseSalary)
    88     const s = parseFloat(sickDays)
    89     const w = parseFloat(workingDays)
    90     const y = parseFloat(workYears)
    91     if (!b || !s || !w) return null
    92     return calcSickWage({ baseSalary: b, sickDays: s, workingDays: w, workYears: y || 0 })
    93   }, [baseSalary, sickDays, workingDays, workYears])
    94 
    95   const penaltyResult = useMemo(() => {
    96     const m = parseFloat(monthlyRent)
    97     const r = parseFloat(remainMonths)
    98     const c = parseFloat(contractMonths)
    99     const v = parseFloat(penaltyValue)
   100     if (!m || !r || !v) return null
   101     return calcPenalty({ monthlyRent: m, contractMonths: c || 0, remainMonths: r, penaltyType, penaltyValue: v })
   102   }, [monthlyRent, contractMonths, remainMonths, penaltyType, penaltyValue])
   103

   117             onClick={() => setActiveTab(tab.key)}
   118           >
   119             <div className={`${tab.icon} text-2xl ${activeTab === tab.key ? 'text-primary' : 'text-muted-foreground'}`} />
   120             <span className={`text-xl font-medium ${activeTab === tab.key ? 'text-primary' : 'text-muted-foreground'}`}>{tab.label}</span>
   121           </div>
   122         ))}
   123       </div>
   124 
   125       <div className="px-4 py-4">
   126         {/* 病假工资计算器 */}
   127         {activeTab === 'sick' && (
   128           <div>
   129             <div className="bg-card rounded-2xl border border-border p-4 mb-4">
   130               <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground mb-4">病假工资计算</p>
   131               <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
   132                 {[
   133                   { label: '月基本工资（元）', value: baseSalary, setter: setBaseSalary, placeholder: '请输入月基本工资', required: true },
   134                   { label: '病假天数（天）', value: sickDays, setter: setSickDays, placeholder: '请输入病假天数', required: true },
   135                   { label: '月计薪天数（天）', value: workingDays, setter: setWorkingDays, placeholder: '一般为21.75天', required: true },
   136                   { label: '工作年限（年）', value: workYears, setter: setWorkYears, placeholder: '影响病假工资比例', required: false },
   137                 ].map(({ label, value, setter, placeholder, required }) => (
   138                   <div key={label}>

   144                       <input

   148                         value={value}
   149                         onInput={(e) => { const ev = e as any; setter(ev.detail?.value ?? ev.target?.value ?? '') }}
   150                       />
   151                     </div>
   152                   </div>
   153                 ))}
   154               </div>
   155             </div>
   156 
   157             {/* 工龄参照表 */}
   158             <div className="bg-secondary rounded-2xl p-4 mb-4">
   159               <p className="text-xl font-medium text-foreground mb-3">病假工资系数参照（上海标准）</p>
   160               {[
   161                 ['工龄不满2年', '60%'],
   162                 ['工龄满2年不满5年', '70%'],
   163                 ['工龄满5年不满10年', '80%'],
   164                 ['工龄满10年不满20年', '90%'],
   165                 ['工龄满20年及以上', '100%'],
   166               ].map(([years, ratio]) => (

   168                   <span className="text-xl text-foreground">{years}</span>
   169                   <span className="text-xl font-medium text-primary">{ratio}</span>
   170                 </div>
   171               ))}
   172             </div>
   173 
   174             {sickResult && sickResult.result > 0 && (
   175               <div className="bg-card rounded-2xl border border-primary p-4">
   176                 <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground mb-2">计算结果</p>
   177                 <div className="flex items-baseline gap-2 mb-3">
   178                   <span className="text-3xl font-bold text-primary">{sickResult.result.toFixed(2)}</span>
   179                   <span className="text-xl text-muted-foreground">元</span>
   180                 </div>
   181                 <div className="law-quote">
   182                   <p className="text-xl text-foreground leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-line">{sickResult.detail}</p>
   183                 </div>
   184               </div>
   185             )}
   186           </div>
   187         )}
   188 
   189         {/* 违约金计算器 */}
   190         {activeTab === 'penalty' && (
   191           <div>
   192             <div className="bg-card rounded-2xl border border-border p-4 mb-4">
   193               <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground mb-4">租房违约金计算</p>
   194               <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
   195                 {[
   196                   { label: '月租金（元）', value: monthlyRent, setter: setMonthlyRent, placeholder: '请输入月租金金额', required: true },
   197                   { label: '合同租期（月）', value: contractMonths, setter: setContractMonths, placeholder: '如：12', required: false },
   198                   { label: '剩余租期（月）', value: remainMonths, setter: setRemainMonths, placeholder: '提前退租的剩余月数', required: true },
   199                 ].map(({ label, value, setter, placeholder, required }) => (
   200                   <div key={label}>
   201                     <div className="flex items-center gap-1 mb-2">
   202                       <span className="text-xl text-foreground">{label}</span>
   203                       {required && <span className="text-xl text-destructive">*</span>}
   204                     </div>
   205                     <div className="border border-input rounded-lg px-4 py-3 bg-background overflow-hidden">
   206                       <input
   207                         type="digit"
   208                         className="w-full text-xl text-foreground bg-transparent outline-none"
   209                         placeholder={placeholder}
   210                         value={value}
   211                         onInput={(e) => { const ev = e as any; setter(ev.detail?.value ?? ev.target?.value ?? '') }}
   212                       />
   213                     </div>
   214                   </div>
   215                 ))}
   216 
   217                 <div>
   218                   <p className="text-xl text-foreground mb-2">违约金计算方式</p>
   219                   <div className="flex gap-3">
   220                     {[

   222                       { type: 'fixed' as const, label: '固定金额' },
   223                     ].map(opt => (
   224                       <div
   225                         key={opt.type}
   226                         className={`flex-1 py-3 rounded-xl border text-center text-xl transition-all ${penaltyType === opt.type ? 'border-primary bg-secondary text-primary' : 'border-border bg-background text-foreground'}`}
   227                         onClick={() => setPenaltyType(opt.type)}
   228                       >
   229                         {opt.label}
   230                       </div>
   231                     ))}
   232                   </div>
   233                 </div>
   234

   239                   </p>

   241                     <input
   242                       type="digit"

   244                       placeholder={penaltyType === 'ratio' ? '如：2（表示2个月租金）' : '请输入固定违约金金额'}
   245                       value={penaltyValue}
   246                       onInput={(e) => { const ev = e as any; setPenaltyValue(ev.detail?.value ?? ev.target?.value ?? '') }}
   247                     />
   248                   </div>
   249                 </div>
   250               </div>
   251             </div>
   252 
   253             {penaltyResult && penaltyResult.result > 0 && (

     7 /** 调用 Embedding API 获取查询向量（失败时静默返回 null，不阻断正常对话） */
     8 async function getQueryEmbedding(text: string, apiKey: string): Promise<number[] | null> {
     9   try {
    10     const response = await fetch(EMBED_API, {
    11       method: 'POST',
    12       headers: {
    13         'Content-Type': 'application/json',
    14         'X-Gateway-Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
    15       },
    16       body: JSON.stringify({ model: 'text-embedding-3-small', input: text, dimensions: 1024 }),
    17       signal: AbortSignal.timeout(8000), // 8 秒超时，避免阻塞整体流程
    18     })
    19     if (!response.ok) return null
    20     const data = await response.json()
    21     const embedding = data?.data?.[0]?.embedding
    22     return Array.isArray(embedding) ? embedding : null
    23   } catch {
    24     return null
    25   }
    26 }

    28 /** 从知识库检索与问题最相关的法律条文 */
    29 async function searchLegalDocs(
    30   query: string,
    31   apiKey: string,
    32   supabaseUrl: string,
    33   serviceKey: string
    34 ): Promise<{ title: string; source: string; content: string }[]> {
    35   const embedding = await getQueryEmbedding(query, apiKey)
    36   if (!embedding) return []
    37 
    38   try {

    41       query_embedding: `[${embedding.join(',')}]`,
    42       match_count: 3,
    43       min_similarity: 0.5,
    44     })
    45     if (error || !data) return []
    46     return (data as { title: string; source: string; content: string }[])
    47   } catch {
    48     return []
    49   }

    58 
    59 ---法律依据---

   103 Deno.serve(async (req) => {
   104   if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
   105     return new Response(null, { headers: corsHeaders })
   106   }
   107 
   108   try {
   109     const apiKey = Deno.env.get('INTEGRATIONS_API_KEY')
   110     if (!apiKey) {
   111       return new Response(
   112         JSON.stringify({ error: '服务配置错误，请联系管理员' }),
   113         { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } }
   114       )
   115     }
   116 
   117     const { messages, mode } = await req.json()
   118 
   119     if (!messages || !Array.isArray(messages) || messages.length === 0) {
   120       return new Response(
   121         JSON.stringify({ error: '请提供对话消息' }),
   122         { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } }
   123       )
   124     }
   125 
   126     // 仅在法律咨询模式下执行 RAG 检索（文书生成/博弈模式不需要）
   127     let ragContext = ''
   128     if (mode !== 'document' && mode !== 'dispute') {
   129       const userQuery = messages[messages.length - 1]?.content ?? ''
   130       const supabaseUrl = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL')!
   131       const serviceKey = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY')!
   132       const ragDocs = await searchLegalDocs(userQuery, apiKey, supabaseUrl, serviceKey)
   133       if (ragDocs.length > 0) {
   134         ragContext = '\n\n【知识库检索结果 - 请优先基于以下法律条文回答】\n' +
   135           ragDocs.map((d, i) =>
   136             `${i + 1}. ${d.source || d.title}\n${d.content}`
   137           ).join('\n\n')
   138       }
   139     }
   140 
   141     // 根据模式选择系统提示词，并注入 RAG 上下文
   142     const systemPrompt = (mode === 'document' ? DOCUMENT_SYSTEM_PROMPT
   143       : mode === 'dispute' ? DISPUTE_SYSTEM_PROMPT
   144       : LEGAL_SYSTEM_PROMPT) + ragContext
   145 
   146     const apiMessages = [
   147       { role: 'system', content: systemPrompt },
   148       ...messages.map((m: { role: string; content: string }) => ({
   149         role: m.role,
   150         content: m.content,
   151       }))
   152     ]
   153 
   154     // 从环境变量读取模型名，默认使用 ernie-lite-8k
   155     const modelName = Deno.env.get('CHAT_MODEL') || 'ernie-lite-8k'
   156 
   157     const response = await fetch(TEXT_API, {
   158       method: 'POST',
   159       headers: {
   160         'Content-Type': 'application/json',
   161         'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
   162         'X-Gateway-Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
   163       },
   164       body: JSON.stringify({
   165         model: modelName,
   166         messages: apiMessages,
   167         stream: false, // 关闭流式，直接返回完整 JSON，避免网关 504 超时
   168       }),
   169       signal: AbortSignal.timeout(55000), // 55 秒全局超时保护
   170     })
   171 
   172     if (!response.ok) {
   173       const errText = await response.text()
   174       console.error(`文本API错误 [${response.status}]:`, errText)
   175       if (response.status === 429) {
   176         return new Response(
   177           JSON.stringify({ error: '请求过于频繁，请稍后再试' }),
   178           { status: 429, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } }
   179         )
   180       }
   181       if (response.status === 401 || response.status === 403) {
   182         return new Response(
   183           JSON.stringify({ error: 'API密钥无效，请联系管理员' }),
   184           { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } }
   185         )
   186       }
   187       if (response.status === 402) {
   188         return new Response(
   189           JSON.stringify({ error: 'API余额不足，请联系管理员' }),
   190           { status: 402, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } }
   191         )
   192       }
   193       if (response.status === 400) {
   194         return new Response(
   195           JSON.stringify({ error: '请求参数错误，请检查输入内容' }),
   196           { status: 400, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } }
   197         )
   198       }
   199       return new Response(
   200         JSON.stringify({ error: 'AI服务暂时不可用，请稍后再试' }),
   201         { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } }
   202       )
   203     }
   204 
   205     // 非流式响应：直接解析完整 JSON
   206     const respData = await response.json()
   207     const fullContent: string = respData?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content
   208       || respData?.choices?.[0]?.delta?.content
   209       || ''
   210 
   211     return new Response(
   212       JSON.stringify({ content: fullContent, rag_used: ragContext.length > 0 }),
   213       { headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } }
   214     )
   215   } catch (error) {
   216     console.error('法律咨询错误:', error)
   217     return new Response(
   218       JSON.stringify({ error: '服务异常，请稍后重试' }),
   219       { status: 500, headers: { ...corsHeaders, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } }
   220     )
   221   }

--BEGIN AGENT OBSERVATION--
import Taro from '@tarojs/taro'

interface CallEdgeFunctionOptions {
  body?: unknown
  method?: 'GET' | 'POST' | 'PUT' | 'DELETE'
  headers?: Record<string, string>
}

interface CallEdgeFunctionResult<T = unknown> {
  data: T | null
  error: { message: string } | null
}

/**
 * 统一调用 Supabase Edge Function 的工具函数。
 *
 * 背景：supabase.functions.invoke 内部经过 customFetch → Taro.request 传递时，
 * body 序列化存在兼容问题，导致 WeChat 小程序环境下请求无法发出。
 * 同时 Taro.request 在 H5（浏览器）模式下 fail 回调行为异常，故 H5 用原生 fetch，
 * WeChat 小程序用 Taro.request，两套路径均绕过 supabase.functions.invoke。
 */
export function callEdgeFunction<T = unknown>(
  functionName: string,
  options: CallEdgeFunctionOptions = {}
): Promise<CallEdgeFunctionResult<T>> {
  const { body, method = 'POST', headers = {} } = options
  const url = `${process.env.TARO_APP_SUPABASE_URL}/functions/v1/${functionName}`
  const anonKey = process.env.TARO_APP_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY || ''
  const reqHeaders: Record<string, string> = {
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
    'Authorization': `Bearer ${anonKey}`,
    'apikey': anonKey,
    ...headers,
  }
  const reqBody = body !== undefined ? JSON.stringify(body) : undefined

  // H5（浏览器）环境：直接用原生 fetch，避免 Taro.request 在 H5 下 fail 回调异常
  if (Taro.getEnv() === Taro.ENV_TYPE.WEB) {
    return fetch(url, { method, headers: reqHeaders, body: reqBody })
      .then(async (res) => {
        const parsed = await res.json().catch(() => null)
        if (res.ok) return { data: parsed as T, error: null }
        const msg = (parsed as Record<string, unknown>)?.error
          || (parsed as Record<string, unknown>)?.message
          || `HTTP ${res.status}`
        return { data: null, error: { message: String(msg) } }
      })
      .catch((err: unknown) => ({
        data: null,
        error: { message: (err as Error)?.message || '网络请求失败' },
      }))
  }

  // WeChat 小程序环境：使用 Taro.request，避免 customFetch 的 body 序列化问题
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    Taro.request({
      url,
      method,
      header: reqHeaders,
      data: reqBody,
      success(res) {
        const parsed = typeof res.data === 'string'
          ? (() => { try { return JSON.parse(res.data) } catch { return res.data } })()
          : res.data
        if (res.statusCode >= 200 && res.statusCode < 300) {
          resolve({ data: parsed as T, error: null })
        } else {
          const p = parsed as Record<string, unknown> | null
          const msg = p?.error || p?.message || `HTTP ${res.statusCode}`
          resolve({ data: null, error: { message: String(msg) } })
        }
      },
      fail(err) {
        resolve({ data: null, error: { message: err.errMsg || '网络请求失败' } })
      },
    })
  })
}

API gateway 可能使用不同的认证方式\n\n让我查看是否有任何关于TEXT_API的信息。URL是：\n`https://app-bar9rto6gwsh-api-zYkZz8qovQ1L-gateway.appmiaoda.com/v2/chat/completions`\n\n这是一个通过秒哒(Miaoda)网关访问AI的API。这个gateway通常只需要 `X-Gateway-Authorization` 头，不需要 `Authorization` 头，并且也许不需要 model 参数（因为gateway可能自动选择模型）。\n\n实际上，我怀疑添加 `Authorization: Bearer ${apiKey}` header可能干扰了gateway的认证，导致出现了401/403错误，进而返回了我们的错误提示。\n\n之前的代码只有 `X-Gateway-Authorization: Bearer ${apiKey}`，但我们改成了同时发送两个header：\n- `Authorization: Bearer ${apiKey}`\n- `X-Gateway-Authorization: Bearer ${apiKey}`\n\n某些API网关如果同时收到两个认证头，可能会出现冲突。\n\n另外，`model` 参数可能也是问题所在：如果gateway有自己的模型映射，前端传 `ernie-lite-8k` 可能不是正确的模型名称。\n\n但更关键的是，上次修复的版本（v21）已经部署了，截图应该是v21之后的问题。\n\n让我思考：\n- v20之前的代码没有 model 参数，会导致API返回400 Bad Request（missing required field `model`）\n- v21添加了 model: \'ernie-lite-8k\'，但这个模型名可能不被支持，导致另一种错误\n\n更可能的问题是：调用 Miaoda 平台的 gateway API，需要特定的模型名称。\'ernie-lite-8k\'是百度文心一言的模型名，但通过Miaoda网关可能需要不同的名称。\n\n但是我无法确认正确的模型名称，因为我没有访问该API文档的权限。\n\n让我从另一个角度考虑：\n1. 原始代码没有model参数 → 可能API需要模型参数\n2. 添加了model参数后→ 是否就解决了问题？\n\n实际上，根据截图，看起来这个问题是在v21部署后才出现的。用户提问"文书生成部分出现问题"，截图显示咨询也失败了。\n\n我需要检查：\n1. 是否有更合适的模型名称\n2. 检查API调用路径是否有其他问题\n\n看看`/workspace/app-bar9rto6gwsh/src/pages/document/index.tsx`的最新状态，因为上次的memorized context中有大量的document修改，而最终效果尚不清楚。\n\n让我先看document页面的当前状态。\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

    84 function parseDisputeReply(content: string) {
    85   const argsMatch = content.match(/---对方可能的狡辩---([\s\S]*?)(?=---|$)/)
    86   const counterMatch = content.match(/---学长教你怎么拆招---([\s\S]*?)(?=---|$)/)
    87   return {
    88     args: argsMatch ? argsMatch[1].trim() : content,
    89     counter: counterMatch ? counterMatch[1].trim() : '',
    90   }
    91 }
    92 
    93 export default function Documents() {
    94   // 从 URL 参数读取当前步骤和选中模版
    95   const routerParams = useMemo(() => {
    96     const instance = Taro.getCurrentInstance()
    97     return instance?.router?.params || {}
    98   }, [])
    99 
   100   const currentStep = useMemo(() => routerParams.step || 'list', [routerParams])
   101   const templateId = useMemo(() => routerParams.templateId || '', [routerParams])
   102 
   103   // 根据 URL 参数中的 templateId 查找模版
   104   const selectedTemplate = useMemo(() => {
   105     if (!templateId) return null
   106     return TEMPLATES.find(t => t.id === templateId) || null
   107   }, [templateId])
   108 
   109   const [formData, setFormData] = useState<Record<string, string>>({})
   110   const [generating, setGenerating] = useState(false)
   111   const [generatedDoc, setGeneratedDoc] = useState(() => {
   112     // 从 storage 恢复生成的文书（结果步骤时读取）
   113     if (currentStep === 'result') {
   114       try { return Taro.getStorageSync('document_result') || '' } catch { return '' }
   115     }
   116     return ''
   117   })
   118   const [disputeContent, setDisputeContent] = useState('')
   119   const [loadingDispute, setLoadingDispute] = useState(false)
   120   const [showDispute, setShowDispute] = useState(false)
   121 
   122   const setField = (key: string, value: string) => {
   123     setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, [key]: value }))
   124   }
   125 
   126   const handleGenerate = useCallback(async () => {
   127     if (!selectedTemplate) return
   128     const missingFields = selectedTemplate.fields
   129       .filter(f => f.required && !formData[f.key]?.trim())
   130       .map(f => f.label)
   131 
   132     if (missingFields.length > 0) {
   133       Taro.showToast({ title: `请填写：${missingFields[0]}`, icon: 'none' })
   134       return
   135     }
   136 
   137     setGenerating(true)
   138     try {
   139       const fieldStr = selectedTemplate.fields
   140         .map(f => `${f.label}：${formData[f.key] || '（未填写）'}`)
   141         .join('\n')
   142 
   143       const prompt = `${selectedTemplate.prompt}\n${fieldStr}\n\n请生成完整规范的法律文书，格式清晰，符合法律规范。`
   144 
   145       const { data, error } = await callEdgeFunction<{ content?: string }>('legal-chat', {
   146         body: { messages: [{ role: 'user', content: prompt }], mode: 'document' },
   147       })
   148 
   149       if (error) {
   150         console.error('文书生成错误:', error.message)
   151         Taro.showToast({ title: '生成失败，请稍后重试', icon: 'none' })
   152         return
   153       }
   154       const doc = data?.content || ''
   155       // 将结果存入 storage，再跳转到结果页
   156       Taro.setStorageSync('document_result', doc)
   157       Taro.setStorageSync('document_template_name', selectedTemplate.name)
   158       // redirectTo 替换当前表单页，跳转到结果页
   159       Taro.redirectTo({ url: `/pages/document/index?step=result&templateId=${selectedTemplate.id}` })
   160     } catch {
   161       Taro.showToast({ title: '网络异常，请稍后重试', icon: 'none' })
   162     } finally {
   163       setGenerating(false)
   164     }
   165   }, [selectedTemplate, formData])
   166 
   167   const handleSimulateDispute = useCallback(async () => {
   168     if (!generatedDoc) return
   169     const templateName = Taro.getStorageSync('document_template_name') || '法律文书'
   170     setLoadingDispute(true)
   171     setShowDispute(true)
   172     try {
   173       const prompt = `我已发出以下《${templateName}》：\n\n${generatedDoc.substring(0, 500)}\n\n请模拟对方（房东/雇主/中介）可能的狡辩，并教我如何拆招。`
   174       const { data, error } = await callEdgeFunction<{ content?: string }>('legal-chat', {
   175         body: { messages: [{ role: 'user', content: prompt }], mode: 'dispute' },
   176       })
   177       if (error) {
   178         Taro.showToast({ title: '模拟失败，请重试', icon: 'none' })
   179         setShowDispute(false)
   180         return
   181       }
   182       setDisputeContent(data?.content || '')
   183     } catch {
   184       Taro.showToast({ title: '网络异常，请稍后重试', icon: 'none' })
   185       setShowDispute(false)
   186     } finally {
   187       setLoadingDispute(false)
   188     }
   189   }, [generatedDoc])
   190 
   191   const copyDoc = () => {
   192     Taro.setClipboardData({
   193       data: generatedDoc,
   194       success: () => Taro.showToast({ title: '已复制到剪贴板', icon: 'success' }),
   195     })
   196   }
   197 
   198   const goBackToList = () => {
   199     // 清除缓存并返回模版列表
   200     Taro.removeStorageSync('document_result')
   201     Taro.removeStorageSync('document_template_name')
   202     Taro.navigateBack({ delta: 99 })
   203   }
   204 
   205   const disputeParsed = disputeContent ? parseDisputeReply(disputeContent) : null
   206 
   207   // 结果页面
   208   if (currentStep === 'result') {
   209     const templateName = Taro.getStorageSync('document_template_name') || '法律文书'
   210     return (
   211       <div className="min-h-screen bg-background">
   212         <div className="px-4 py-4">
   213           <div className="bg-card rounded-2xl border border-border p-4 mb-4">
   214             <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
   215               <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground">生成结果</p>
   216               <span className="text-xl px-2 py-1 bg-secondary text-primary rounded">{templateName}</span>
   217             </div>
   218             <div className="border border-border rounded-xl p-4 bg-background">
   219               <p className="text-xl text-foreground leading-loose whitespace-pre-wrap">{generatedDoc}</p>
   220             </div>
   221           </div>
   222 
   223           {!showDispute && (
   224             <button
   225               type="button"
   226               className="flex items-center justify-center leading-none gap-2 border border-primary bg-background rounded-xl w-full mb-3"
   227               onClick={handleSimulateDispute}
   228             >
   229               <div className="py-4 flex items-center gap-2">
   230                 <div className="i-mdi-shield-sword-outline text-2xl text-primary" />
   231                 <span className="text-xl text-primary">学长模拟：对方会怎么狡辩？</span>
   232               </div>
   233             </button>
   234           )}
   235 
   236           {showDispute && (
   237             <div className="bg-card rounded-2xl border border-border mb-4 overflow-hidden">
   238               <div className="flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-3 border-b border-border">
   239                 <div className="i-mdi-sword-cross text-xl text-primary" />
   240                 <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground">见招拆招</p>
   241               </div>
   242               {loadingDispute ? (
   243                 <div className="p-4 flex flex-col gap-2">
   244                   <div className="skeleton h-4 rounded" />
   245                   <div className="skeleton h-4 rounded w-5/6" />
   246                   <div className="skeleton h-4 rounded w-4/6" />
   247                 </div>
   248               ) : disputeParsed && (
   249                 <div className="p-4 flex flex-col gap-4">
   250                   <div>
   251                     <p className="text-xl font-medium text-destructive mb-2">对方可能的狡辩</p>
   252                     <p className="text-xl text-foreground leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-wrap">{disputeParsed.args}</p>
   253                   </div>
   254                   {disputeParsed.counter && (
   255                     <div>
   256                       <p className="text-xl font-medium text-primary mb-2">学长教你怎么拆招</p>
   257                       <div className="law-quote">
   258                         <p className="text-xl text-foreground leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-wrap">{disputeParsed.counter}</p>
   259                       </div>
   260                     </div>
   261                   )}
   262                 </div>
   263               )}
   264             </div>
   265           )}
   266 
   267           <div className="flex flex-col gap-3">
   268             <button
   269               type="button"
   270               className="flex items-center justify-center leading-none gap-2 bg-primary rounded-xl"
   271               onClick={copyDoc}
   272             >
   273               <div className="py-4 flex items-center gap-2">
   274                 <div className="i-mdi-content-copy text-2xl text-primary-foreground" />
   275                 <span className="text-xl text-primary-foreground">复制文书内容</span>
   276               </div>
   277             </button>
   278             <button
   279               type="button"
   280               className="flex items-center justify-center leading-none gap-2 border border-border bg-background rounded-xl"
   281               onClick={goBackToList}
   282             >
   283               <div className="py-4 flex items-center gap-2">
   284                 <div className="i-mdi-refresh text-2xl text-foreground" />
   285                 <span className="text-xl text-foreground">重新选择模板</span>
   286               </div>
   287             </button>
   288           </div>
   289           <div className="mt-4 flex items-start gap-2 px-4 py-3 bg-muted rounded-xl">
   290             <div className="i-mdi-information-outline text-xl text-muted-foreground flex-shrink-0 mt-0.5" />
   291             <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">本回复由AI生成，仅供参考，不构成正式法律建议。若情况紧急请咨询专业律师。</p>
   292           </div>
   293         </div>
   294       </div>
   295     )
   296   }
   297 
   298   // 表单填写页面
   299   if (currentStep === 'form' && selectedTemplate) {
   300     return (
   301       <div className="min-h-screen bg-background">
   302         <div className="px-4 py-4">
   303           <div className="bg-card rounded-2xl border border-border p-4 mb-4">
   304             <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-4">
   305               <div className={`${selectedTemplate.icon} text-3xl text-primary`} />
   306               <div>
   307                 <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground">{selectedTemplate.name}</p>
   308                 <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground">{selectedTemplate.desc}</p>
   309               </div>
   310             </div>
   311             <div className="flex flex-col gap-4">
   312               {selectedTemplate.fields.map((field) => (
   313                 <div key={field.key}>
   314                   <div className="flex items-center gap-1 mb-2">
   315                     <span className="text-xl text-foreground">{field.label}</span>
   316                     {field.required && <span className="text-xl text-destructive">*</span>}
   317                   </div>
   318                   <div className="border border-input rounded-lg px-4 py-3 bg-background overflow-hidden">
   319                     <input
   320                       className="w-full text-xl text-foreground bg-transparent outline-none"
   321                       placeholder={field.placeholder}
   322                       value={formData[field.key] || ''}
   323                       onInput={(e) => { const ev = e as any; setField(field.key, ev.detail?.value ?? ev.target?.value ?? '') }}
   324                     />
   325                   </div>
   326                 </div>
   327               ))}
   328             </div>
   329           </div>
   330           <div className="flex flex-col gap-3">
   331             <button
   332               type="button"
   333               className="flex items-center justify-center leading-none bg-primary rounded-xl"
   334               style={{ opacity: generating ? 0.5 : 1 }}
   335               onClick={handleGenerate}
   336             >
   337               <div className="py-4 flex items-center gap-2">
   338                 {generating ? (
   339                   <div className="i-mdi-loading text-2xl text-primary-foreground animate-spin" />
   340                 ) : (
   341                   <div className="i-mdi-file-document-edit-outline text-2xl text-primary-foreground" />
   342                 )}
   343                 <span className="text-xl text-primary-foreground">{generating ? '生成中...' : '生成文书'}</span>
   344               </div>
   345             </button>
   346             <button
   347               type="button"
   348               className="flex items-center justify-center leading-none border border-border bg-background rounded-xl"
   349               onClick={() => Taro.navigateBack()}
   350             >
   351               <div className="py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
   352                 <div className="i-mdi-arrow-left text-2xl text-foreground" />
   353                 <span className="text-xl text-foreground">返回选择模板</span>
   354               </div>
   355             </button>
   356           </div>
   357         </div>
   358       </div>
   359     )
   360   }
   361 
   362   // 模板选择页面（默认）
   363   return (
   364     <div className="min-h-screen bg-background">
   365       <div className="px-4 py-4">
   366         <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground mb-4">选择需要生成的文书类型</p>
   367         <div className="flex flex-col gap-3">
   368           {TEMPLATES.map((template) => (
   369             <div
   370               key={template.id}
   371               className="bg-card rounded-2xl border border-border p-4 flex items-center gap-4 transition-all active:scale-95"
   372               onClick={() => Taro.navigateTo({ url: `/pages/document/index?step=form&templateId=${template.id}` })}
   373             >
   374               <div className={`${template.icon} text-3xl text-primary flex-shrink-0`} />
   375               <div className="flex-1">
   376                 <p className="text-xl font-semibold text-foreground">{template.name}</p>
   377                 <p className="text-xl text-muted-foreground mt-1">{template.desc}</p>
   378               </div>
   379               <div className="i-mdi-chevron-right text-2xl text-muted-foreground" />
   380             </div>
   381           ))}
   382         </div>
   383       </div>
   384     </div>
   385   )
   386 }
